  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0874cd2d-d398-4641-88a5-68a9346a0bee'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer9731133892754548311">Book 3 of the After series—newly revised and expanded, Anna Todd's After fanfiction racked up 1 billion reads online and captivated readers across the globe. Experience the internet's most talked-about book for yourself from the writer Cosmopolitan called “the biggest literary phenomenon of her generation.”<br/><br/>Tessa and Hardin’s love was complicated before. Now it’s more confu</span>
  <span id="freeText9731133892754548311" style="display:none">Book 3 of the After series—newly revised and expanded, Anna Todd's After fanfiction racked up 1 billion reads online and captivated readers across the globe. Experience the internet's most talked-about book for yourself from the writer Cosmopolitan called “the biggest literary phenomenon of her generation.”<br /><br />Tessa and Hardin’s love was complicated before. Now it’s more confusing than ever. AFTER WE FELL...Life will never be the same. #HESSA<br /><br />Just as Tessa makes the biggest decision of her life, everything changes. Revelations about first her family, and then Hardin’s, throw everything they knew before in doubt and makes their hard-won future together more difficult to claim.<br /><br />Tessa’s life begins to come unglued. Nothing is what she thought it was. Not her friends. Not her family. The one person she should be able to rely on, Hardin, is furious when he discovers the massive secret she’s been keeping. And rather than being understanding, he turns to sabotage.<br /><br />Tessa knows Hardin loves her and will do anything to protect her, but there’s a difference between loving someone and being able to have them in your life. This cycle of jealousy, unpredictable anger, and forgiveness is exhausting. She’s never felt so intensely for anyone, so exhilarated by someone’s kiss—but is the irrepressible heat between her and Hardin worth all the drama? Love used to be enough to hold them together. But if Tessa follows her heart now, will it be...the end?</span>
  <a data-text-id="9731133892754548311" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

  <span id="freeText13226969415026239635" style="display:none">This is a flipping adolescent version of Fifty Shades of Grey. <br><br>Except it's featuring Harry Styles. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390248028ra/8175971.gif" width="499" height="267" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Now that we've covered that, let's get going with this shit review. <br><br>So, how about we go through an overview of what the trilogy looked like to me:<br><br>Tessa (who has like three different names) is gorgeous, curvy, blonde, funny, innocent, and has all of the charming characteristics every female protagonist on Wattpad has. <div id="review_2061356354" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2061356354" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2061356354?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22813717-after-we-fell">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2061356354" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7124234506201093393">Like the first two books in the series, 'After We Fell' was completely consuming. Although the back and forth drama between Hardin and Tessa gets to be very irritating, I can't seem to turn away from it. It's like I'm stuck in an abusive relationship with this couple. I know it isn't healthy. I know I should remove myself from the situation...but I just can't do it. After all, maybe they'll change.<br/><br/>Picking up where 'After We Collided' left off, Tessa's father has reappeared in her life. Only, her</span>
  <span id="freeText7124234506201093393" style="display:none">Like the first two books in the series, 'After We Fell' was completely consuming. Although the back and forth drama between Hardin and Tessa gets to be very irritating, I can't seem to turn away from it. It's like I'm stuck in an abusive relationship with this couple. I know it isn't healthy. I know I should remove myself from the situation...but I just can't do it. After all, maybe they'll change.<br /><br />Picking up where 'After We Collided' left off, Tessa's father has reappeared in her life. Only, her father is not the man that she remembered from her childhood. He is homeless and has some serious addiction issues. <br /><br />While Tessa wants to give her father a chance, Hardin cautions her against it. Hardin is an ass all of the time, but I really thought that he took it to a whole new level when her father was introduced. I couldn't believe how incredibly insensitive and cruel he was. Even though he was absolutely correct to be concerned, he responded in a manner that showed absolutely no regard for Tessa's feelings. I couldn't believe some of the things he said about her father to her. Of course, like always, Tessa gets over it like it was hardly a blip on her radar.<br /><br />More than the first two books, Hardin's own issues with addiction were very apparent. Interestingly, the author seemed to avoid addressing this issue head on. I kept waiting for some sort of intervention, but it never really happened. I guess there was already enough drama in this story without tackling Hardin's drinking problem.<br /><br />This book also features plenty of fighting, breaking up and making up between Hardin and Tessa. If you expected Hardin and Tessa to settle down and start acting like a mature, committed couple, prepare to be disappointed. 'After We Fell' is full of the same angst-filled cycle of jealousy, acting out and game playing that were in previous books. Betrayals are around every corner and there is no shortage of drama.<br /><br />From disastrous family vacations, to secrets, there is plenty of deceit to go around. Zed is back on scene again, playing a big role in the tension between Hardin and Tessa. Of course, he is only involved because Tessa pulled him in again. Meanwhile, there are more revelations about Tessa's "friends". I swear, they never learn their lessons!<br /><br />Like the first two books, this book ends with a huge upset. If I ever thought that I would have the strength to quit this dysfunctional couple, the ending sucked me right back in. I absolutely had to see where the next book would lead. <br /><br />I love to hate, and hate to love, this series! It is like watching a bad train wreck in slow motion. You know it's going to be a disaster, but you just can't turn away.<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="7124234506201093393" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13295052892680286013" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499324550i/23216915._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495397142ra/22813203.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499324550ra/23216916.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499324550ra/23216917.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️1/2! After We Fell, book 3 of 5. The tumultuous against-all-odds romance between tatted rebel Hardin Scott &amp; good girl Tessa Young!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“There is a big difference between not being able to live without someone and loving them.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><u>Books in The After series should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090449623" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1952340915" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Collided</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1994022284" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Fell</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2000467437" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After Ever Happy</a><br>Book 5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2000467456" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Before</a></b><br><br>The After series is the epic love saga between flawed rebel bad boy student and editor <b>Hardin Allen Scott</b> and naïve good girl student and intern editor <b>Theresa Lynn Young, Tessa.</b><br><br><i>In <b>After, book 1-2,</b> Tessa met her polar opposite in Hardin. An unlikely friendship blossomed into a <b>dysfunctional and co-dependent relationship</b> driven by their intense sexual connection.</i><br><br><b>After We Fell, book 3</b> is another chapter of Hardin and Tessa <b>testing and pushing</b> each other. Much stems from immaturity and unresolved issues from their pasts. <br><br>Will Tessa be able to stand up for herself and will Hardin learn to temper his volatile and self-sabotaging side? Or will <b>their love succumb</b> to meddling, jealousy, secrets and betrayal?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496016874ra/22874859.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nine words to describe <b> Hardin Allen Scott:</b> Unpredictable, moody, flawed, broken, aloof, secretive, demanding, conflicted and possessive.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496016874ra/22874860.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nine words to describe <b> Theresa Lynn Young, Tessa:</b> Organized, meek, compulsive, goal-oriented, determined, naïve, trusting, curious and forgiving.<br><br><b>After We Fell,</b> told from dual POVs, is an all-consuming, addicting, at times angsty journey of <b>self-discovery, testing boundaries, pushing limits</b> and <b>surrendering</b> it all for love. It ends leading right to book 4, <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2000467437" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">After Ever Happy</a>

<div id="review_2203752418" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2203752418" />
    <a title="Evgnossia O&#39;Hara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43416866-evgnossia-o-hara"><img alt="Evgnossia O&#39;Hara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537347712p2/43416866.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2203752418?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Evgnossia O&#39;Hara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Evgnossia O&#39;Hara" href="/user/show/43416866-evgnossia-o-hara">Evgnossia O&#39;Hara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2203752418" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer103321429497235604"><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br/><br/>Well, I wasn’t supposed to write a review on the third book of the series due to my highly negative reviews on the two previous books.<br/><br/>And here I am –<b>again</b>-, writing a review-<b>again</b>-, on the After series by Anna Todd –<b>again</b>. It is a vicious circle, just like Hardin’s and Tess’ relationship. Feel the irony?<br/> <br/>I went into this one with very low expectation or to be completely truthful, I expected it to be as horrible as the previous books. And yet, I’ve decided to read it perhaps because I </span>
  <span id="freeText103321429497235604" style="display:none"><b>*3.5 stars*</b><br><br>Well, I wasn’t supposed to write a review on the third book of the series due to my highly negative reviews on the two previous books.<br><br>And here I am –<b>again</b>-, writing a review-<b>again</b>-, on the After series by Anna Todd –<b>again</b>. It is a vicious circle, just like Hardin’s and Tess’ relationship. Feel the irony?<br> <br>I went into this one with very low expectation or to be completely truthful, I expected it to be as horrible as the previous books. And yet, I’ve decided to read it perhaps because I wanted to read something easy and frustrating at the same time, or perhaps, I’m a little bit crazy. Ok, ok, I’m a nut but that is a different story. But most importantly because it was a buddyread with my incredible friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/62576740-mareira" rel="nofollow noopener">Maria</a> who knows how to make you enjoy a book with her humor!<br><br>I won’t say that the pattern changed dramatically. The relationship between those two is completely dysfunctional and unhealthy. Hardin is still a possessive asshole. He’s completely egocentric, selfish with self-esteem issues. Plus Tessa is still an indecisive and a weak-willed woman who cannot stand for herself and become loyal to herself. <br><br>I had internal conversations throughout the story. Again.<br><br><i>Me: Screw Hardin, screw Zed, screw all of them. You are an independent, clever and beautiful woman. So, be that woman! <br><br>Todd: Earth calling…<br><br>Me: Who am I kidding?</i><br><br>Nevertheless, this book was so much better. It took me by surprise. There were two major plot twists that blew my mind away. <br><br>The first one was introduced in the first half of the book. It was completely unexpected, shocking and intimidating. I was screaming and cursing. <br><br><b>
  <i>Out loud.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>At work.</i>
</b><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426053ra/850867.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah… that happened. <br><br>Even though this introduction had a great impact on my reading process, I was skeptical about the second half of the book due to the past unpleasant experiences. I’m glad to say that in total, it wasn’t a disappointment as I thought I would be. There are a lot of fighting, screaming, secrets and of course hot scenes. Very hot…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1513778869ra/24721854.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then again, near to the end Todd gave me another one heart-attack with her cliffhanger and sucked me deeper in the story. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1513778869ra/24721855.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Undoubtedly, this woman knows how to keep the readers invested and make them finish her series. And yes, I’m gonna finish the series because I’m just like Tess who can’t keep her promises when it comes to books and shocking plot twists. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1513778869ra/24721856.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>A small disclaimer:</u><br><br>I still believe that this kind of relationship is a toxic one. They both behave in unpredictable manners, just like psychopaths. I don’t really know how this could end. They just have to end up together or kill each other. There are only these two options. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1513778998ra/24721878.gif" width="" height="" alt="Revenge" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1513778869ra/24721857.gif" width="" height="" alt="What a cliffhanger! Don't you think so?" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>What a cliffhanger! Don't you think so?</i></span>

  <span id="freeText13369369170689944295" style="display:none"><strong>I don’t know why I like it, but I do.</strong><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1579217681ra/28790783.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anna Todd is the queen of the screaming cliffhanger. I don’t even want to wait as long as it will take me to write this review. <br><br>The romance between Hardin and Tessa was unbelievably rocky in the first two books, they spent more time fighting and breaking up than they did happy and together. But in this book, their relationship was on a more even keel, despite the fact that they lived in different cities for much of the book.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> I can’t stop her; she was always meant to do things greater than me, be with someone better than me. I knew that from the start. I was just hoping that somehow I would be wrong, as always.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Also Hardin is really trying to grow up and get his temper under control. Though every now and then he still “sees red” and basically just doesn’t have control and fights and breaks stuff. So he either goes to the gym or focuses his mind on keeping calm when he knows he is about to blow. Which he warns Tessa not to push because he is about to lose it. She knows he would never hurt her, but is afraid that he will end up in jail for assault or property damage.<br><br>This book went deeper into Tessa’s family and Hardin’s background as a bad boy in England as well so that was good, plus the romance between the two was very steamy in this book, though it set up some issues for the future. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1579217681ra/28790782.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://www.instagram.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer2517626627865386357">Audiobook...narrated by Shane East, and Elizabeth Louise. <br/>The narrators were FINE!!!! <br/><br/>Each Audiobook is around 24 hours of listening!!!!<br/><br/>If awards were given for the most ‘eye-rolling’ scrimpy, inconsequential series— these books would win!!! <br/>On that note... I’m still investing my time. <br/>After 3 of these books - ( one more to complete the series)...<br/>Do you want to know my theory as to why I think many of us keep listening to these Audiobooks???..( readers themselves can’t explain the reason fully).</span>
  <span id="freeText2517626627865386357" style="display:none">Audiobook...narrated by Shane East, and Elizabeth Louise. <br />The narrators were FINE!!!! <br /><br />Each Audiobook is around 24 hours of listening!!!!<br /><br />If awards were given for the most ‘eye-rolling’ scrimpy, inconsequential series— these books would win!!! <br />On that note... I’m still investing my time. <br />After 3 of these books - ( one more to complete the series)...<br />Do you want to know my theory as to why I think many of us keep listening to these Audiobooks???..( readers themselves can’t explain the reason fully)...<br />Books that use up hours of meaningless time???<br /><br />The intensity between the unreasonable rage, followed by intense primal passionate sex is kinda fascinating. <br />Who lives like this?? <br /><br />Either the reader has experienced crazy incredible passionate-out of-your-mind-sex - or you haven’t.<br />We are all adults here -( just sayin)...<br />Hardin &amp; Tessa...are definitely not dull-boring- or deadbeat lovers. They might have found the formula that keeps their sex feeling electric.....<br />but the ongoing <br />on and off again fighting would feel too exhausting &amp; scary for most people. <br /><br />I’ve experienced make-up sex... it’s ‘different’...much more intense... and hot. <br />Yet I wouldn’t want the ‘before’ too often in order to experience ‘the after’. <br />I’d selfishly just want the ‘after’ anger sex ( without the anger)...<br /><br />Tessa &amp; Hardin are addicted to each other - it’s rare that their type of relationship would last 70+ hours - as these Audiobooks do. <br /><br />Not many couples could sustain the type of relationship that Tessa and Hardin have. No matter how f#cked up their relationship is - they are both equal partners in keeping their game alive. <br />They give us insights ( yes insights) ... of what a deeply sexual passionate relationship looks like...<br />in order to KEEP THE HEAT HOT.. BURNING HOT...over and over again. <br />....wild &amp; exciting- it’s almost as if this couple is saying...<br />THEIR LOVE FEELS STRONGER as long as fighting is part of what ‘they do’....<br />Each time - they survived the fight - the ‘love’ they feel while having make-up sex is more personal and intense!!! <br /><br />Most of us don’t live with intense lustful - up &amp; down emotions for 1 other person like Tessa and Hardin do. <br /><br />Soo... ‘perhaps’ maybe that’s what many of us find intriguing about these almost - fruitless books. <br /><br />But like I said in my first review of Book 1...<br />Don’t expect me to justify reading them. <br /><br />Book 4 will complete the series. <br />Book 3 was better than book 2. <br />Book 1 was the ‘hook’ that got some of us to continue. <br /><br />Of course I don’t recommend these books ... <br />but I’m enjoying my time with them anyway.</span>

<div id="review_1558128305" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1558128305" />
    <a title="Joana Barros" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36979476-joana-barros"><img alt="Joana Barros" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508537275p2/36979476.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1558128305?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Joana Barros" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Joana Barros" href="/user/show/36979476-joana-barros">Joana Barros</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1558128305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5978523881335447376">I thought this book was never going to end! It has way too many pages. I actually think that book 2 and 3 should merge and become one with half of the pages. There’s a limit for writing the same thing over and over again… The last half of this book was exhausting! It was the same thing over and over again and nothing happens! The scenes in Seattle were so boring! I wish Landon was there to make it better, but no such luck! At least we got that ending. A fucked up ending, but still. So let’s star</span>
  <span id="freeText5978523881335447376" style="display:none">I thought this book was never going to end! It has way too many pages. I actually think that book 2 and 3 should merge and become one with half of the pages. There’s a limit for writing the same thing over and over again… The last half of this book was exhausting! It was the same thing over and over again and nothing happens! The scenes in Seattle were so boring! I wish Landon was there to make it better, but no such luck! At least we got that ending. A fucked up ending, but still. So let’s start with my usual complaints (I’m always complaining about this series). <br /><br />This one is the most important --&gt; Hardin, I already have so many problems with you so don’t add more to the bunch. How can you not like Harry Potter!? You’re a freakin idiot! Just kidding :p But I really hate when people say they don’t like Harry Potter. Just saying... Now, let’s get serious and talk about some specific scenes (some spoilers ahead).<br /><br />This book starts with Tessa getting reacquainted with her dad, who is still a drunk and is also homeless. Tessa takes her dad to her and Hardin’s apartment to feed him and let him rest but he ends up staying there for some days.<br />Meanwhile Hardin finds out about Tessa going to Seattle and he doesn’t like it one bit. He says he’s not going with her but doesn’t come up with a valid reason for it. He just says he doesn’t want to go. They fight a bit, but they stop talking about it because Tessa expects Hardin to change his mind and Hardin expects Tessa to change her mind. Eventually Tessa and Hardin go on a small vacation with Landon, Ken (Hardin’s father) and Karen and that’s where the problems start again.<br /><br />Tessa finds out that Hardin went behind her back and talked to the Seattle real estate agent she contacted, to prevent her from renting an apartment. Tessa is obviously furious because she’s going to Seattle in some days and she doesn’t have an apartment because of Hardin. Going to Seattle while working at a publishing company is her dream since she was a child but Hardin doesn’t care about that. He’s a selfish prick that wants everything to go his way. Thank God, this time, Tessa is so damn furious that she just kicks Hardin out of the room. <br /><br />Hardin gets out of the cabin to take a walk and ends up meeting a girl named Lillian who is also the daughter of one of his father’s college friends, and he talks to her about his problems with Tessa. At one of their conversations something hilarious happens. When he's talking with Lillian at the coffee shop and she tells him that she doesn't hang out with her friends much because her girlfriend doesn't like them and she doesn't want to pick a fight with her, I was like "where does this sound familiar?". And then Hardin goes and says that he thinks her girlfriend is a bitch! I laughed so much! Look at you Hardin, you do the same freakin thing to Tessa! You're a freakin hypocrite! This is unbelievable! But wait, this gets better!<br /><br />I don't know why I still am surprised by Hardin's attitude, but the little stunt he pulled off at the restaurant was so low. He used Lillian (who happens to be a lesbian) to make Tessa jealous, to hurt her when he has already hurt her so much with the story about the Seattle apartment. Before this dinner, Tessa told him she didn't want him to come to Seattle with her since he went behind her back and messed up with her living arrangements. He did that because he doesn't want her to go and leave him, and he’s a moron that doesn't want to go with her for no reason whatsoever. So then he pulls this stunt at the restaurant just to hurt her. She's reaching her breaking point and he just keeps hurting her all over again. He thinks he has the right to mess up with Tessa’s dream but he really doesn't.<br /><br />Obviously, when they get back, Tessa and Hardin fight over all of these things that happened on the trip. Their fight goes to another level this time and they breakup. They say awful things to each other but Tessa still insists with him. She begged him to try again, she begged him to try and change for real this time but he just told her he didn’t want to try anymore. She said that if she left she wouldn’t come back anymore and this time would be for real (I have a hard time believing that, but let’s pretend I believe her). But Hardin just told her to leave and shut the door on her face. <br /><br />Because Hardin and Tessa have broken up, she goes to her supposed go-away (or something like that) party alone. Oh my God, that party! I knew something was going to happen because, let’s face it, there's always something that happens at those frat parties but I didn’t know it was going to be that bad. I though Steph and Molly were going to humiliate Tessa or something because she was the reason for the group splitting up, but <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ drug her, film her and rape her….  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I didn’t expect that. Apparently <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Steph never liked Tessa and has some kind of obsession about Hardin and Dan wanted revenge because of what Hardin did to his sister. Thank God Molly changed her mind and went to get Zed before things escalated to worse. Zed saves Tessa again. He’s always there when she needs him, unlike Hardin. And may I add, that Tessa was going to get hurt again because of Hardin. I’m not blaming him, because Steph is the one to blame here, she’s a psycho, but if it wasn’t for Hardin she wouldn’t be in this situation. Just saying… Well, after this, Zed takes Tessa to her mother’s house because she’s completely drugged and she barely moves and talks. Meanwhile, Molly calls Hardin and tells him what happened. And of course, Hardin goes after Tessa but only after beating the crap out of Dan.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Tessa really gets on my nerves sometimes! Here I was thinking she was finally taking the reins of her life and was going to get herself to a better place after her breakup with Hardin, but no… her resolution of being away from Hardin starts crumbling again. She has an awful night, I know, but that’s not reason to change your mind. She ends up deciding that she wants some time apart from Hardin because he needs to work on his anger and she wants some time to herself. So, they change from a definitive breakup to a pause in the relationship. As you can see, her resolution starts crumbling, again. It doesn’t matter the cruel things Hardin did and told her in their last fights, she is already forgiving him. Hardin ends up agreeing with her and gets back home and Tessa is supposed to leave her mother’s house for Seattle the next morning.<br />But what’s the first thing Tessa does when she gets bored? She calls Hardin! News flash Tessa, if you want some space and don’t want to be so dependent on him you can’t freakin call him all the time! She even asks to call him in the morning! What’s the matter with you, Tessa!? You’re so dependent on Hardin it makes me sick. Do you even remember your last fight with him? What he told you? You’re unbelievable! Can’t you do anything by yourself!? If you want to talk to someone call Landon! He’s your best friend, ffs! Thank God Hardin tells her it’s not a good idea for her to call him in the morning. He actually tells her they shouldn’t call each other while they are apart. Great idea Hardin, I agree with you this time.<br /><br />But then, I have to remind myself that they never do what they’re supposed to do. Hardin and Tessa notion of space is unbelievable! They agreed to take some time apart but they talk on the phone every freakin day of the week for hours! And they barely make in through the week without seeing each other because Hardin gets on his car and drives to Seattle in her first weekend there! Fantastic notion of space! And just like that Tessa forgets everything about their fight, it’s like it never happened! That’s it Tessa, you win! I give up on you! You’re hopeless! You have no self-respect and self-control around Hardin. You love him and I get that but you can’t let him hurt you and crush you over and over again and stay a day mad at him and then kiss him all over his face and everything is fine! This is just ridiculous! But I have my limits, so I’m going to shut up know because I give up! From now on, if you get hurt, I don’t freakin care!<br /><br />Poor Zed goes to Seattle to visit Tessa because he just can’t let her go. Zed maddened Tessa while they went to dinner but he was right. He threw at her some truths about her relationship with Hardin and she didn’t like it. Too bad Tessa, deal with it! I like Zed, but this is getting out of hand. Zed, you have to give up and let her go. She’s obsessed with Hardin and she’s never going to love you like she loves him. <br /><br />Now, Landon. I can’t believe Dakota broke up with him! Why did you do that? He’s perfect! He was going to move to New York because of you! What the hell is he going to do now? He’s so sad it broke my heart. :( I really like Landon and I loved the hug scene where Landon and Tessa are seeing each other again when she’s visiting from Seattle. They really missed each other. I wish they stayed in the same city.<br />And there’s something going on between Ken and Karen but I don’t know what it is.<br /><br />Two things about Hardin that I don’t get at all:<br />1) I really don’t understand how Hardin wanted to move to England when he doesn’t even want Tessa to be there for a weekend. It doesn’t make any sense! <br />2) And what the hell is his problem with marriage? It won’t change anything. You want to be with Tessa forever, you said so yourself, so what’s the problem? If the problem is the divorce, let me tell you that it’s not because of the marriage that people get a divorce. Actually it is because it’s a legal procedure that only happens if people are married, but people break up when they are married and when they are not married. So, being married does not increase the likelihood of Tessa leaving you. I really don’t understand what your problem is.<br /><br />Now the ending of the book. Let’s take a trip down memory lane! Trish (Hardin’s mom) is going to get married to Mike but at the morning of her wedding Hardin catches her <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ kissing Christian Vance. What the hell!? Apparently Trish and Christian have a history that we will only understand in the next book. What I don’t get is why the hell were they kissing when apparently both Trish and Christian love Mike and Kim, respectively. I mean, Trish is supposed to be marrying Mike and Christian is supposed to marry Kim, but they were still kissing!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />But that’s not all! This gets worse! Apparently <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Hardin’s father is Christian and not Ken! Trish cheated on Ken with his best friend! How fucked up is that!? I’m guessing that Ken found out about this and this is the reason why he started drinking.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />I think Hardin is not going to deal with this properly. He trusted <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Christian in a way he didn’t trust Ken and you know how Hardin is with the trusting thing.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> He will probably lash out on Tessa. I just know it. I still can’t believe they kept this secret for years! Dear God, Hardin will never forgive them. After this, I want some explanation for this disclosure. Let’s see what happens in the last book…</span>
  <a data-text-id="5978523881335447376" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1090510578" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090510578" />
    <a title="Ursula Uriarte" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16751097-ursula-uriarte"><img alt="Ursula Uriarte" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467336518p2/16751097.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1090510578?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ursula Uriarte" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ursula Uriarte" href="/user/show/16751097-ursula-uriarte">Ursula Uriarte</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16751097-ursula-uriarte?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16751097-ursula-uriarte?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1090510578" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10765434810871308369">5 stars <br/>(this review contains spoilers for After and After We Collided)<br/><br/>You can check out my review for the rest of the series here:<br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1083143923?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>After</a><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090510702?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>After We Collided</a><br/><br/>The After series keeps on getting better and better! After We Fell is by far my favorite of the three! <br/><br/>At the end of After We Collided we were left again on a cliffhanger with a rather unexpected turn of events, Tessa is trying to find a way to break the news of her impending move to Seattle to Hardin when she runs into her estranged father outs</span>
  <span id="freeText10765434810871308369" style="display:none">5 stars <br>(this review contains spoilers for After and After We Collided)<br><br>You can check out my review for the rest of the series here:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1083143923?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">After</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090510702?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">After We Collided</a><br><br>The After series keeps on getting better and better! After We Fell is by far my favorite of the three! <br><br>At the end of After We Collided we were left again on a cliffhanger with a rather unexpected turn of events, Tessa is trying to find a way to break the news of her impending move to Seattle to Hardin when she runs into her estranged father outside a tattoo shop… <br><br>I hope you guys are fond of rollercoasters because, this book like its two predecessors, is nothing short of one, so hang on tight! <br><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/JimmyRollerCoaster_zpsln2n9okb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420344626ra/13207233.gif" alt=" photo JimmyRollerCoaster_zpsln2n9okb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It’s no surprise when I tell you that as soon as I started I was already frustrated. <br>Tessa is going ahead with her plans to relocate to Seattle with Vance Publishing, Things are rocky with Hardin though not completely called off. <br>Hardin is wayyyyyyyy frustrating though, when one thinks that he is starting to understand that a relationship takes compromise and that it's not all about him and what he wants, he turns into the most unreasonable person ever. He doesn’t have a valid reason at all to not want to move with Tessa to Seattle other than his insecurities, but yet even when he knows this he still chooses to be a total idiot about it. <br>Tessa talks him into coming on a weekend trip with her and his family, in an effort to try and mend things and have some fun together. <br>The trip will prove to be anything but fun! I felt like jumping into the book and screaming at Hardin I just couldn't even process what he was doing!<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/boom%20john%20stewart_zpsrk5e6kta.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420347135ra/13207638.gif" alt=" photo boom john stewart_zpsrk5e6kta.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Once again the Hardin from the past surfaces and it’s like we took 10 steps backward rather than forward, again he proves he can be overly controlling and inconsiderate. I was seriously pissed with him when I found out the lengths that he went to in order to try and get his way. I couldn’t blame Tessa for being tired of his antics, when over and over he screws things up and then expects her to just forgive and forget.<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_m9f2b1RdMO1r7dslf_zps32jnujyf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420346781ra/13207593.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m9f2b1RdMO1r7dslf_zps32jnujyf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/1textashley-benson-caleb-rivers-hanna-marin-pretty-little-liars-tyler-blackburn-Favim.com-232905_zps0z8m0fxm.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420352158ra/13208360.gif" alt=" photo 1textashley-benson-caleb-rivers-hanna-marin-pretty-little-liars-tyler-blackburn-Favim.com-232905_zps0z8m0fxm.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was glad though to see that Tessa didn’t give in to Hardin’s wishes, and put herself and her career first. I think Hardin needs to learn that not everything can go his way. <br>Though while super smart for some things Tessa can be soooo dense for others. She gets invited to a “going away” party at the frat house out of all places. Why would she even consider going there and hanging out with all those people that were nothing but horrible to her? I was screaming at the top of my lungs in frustration, ok fine maybe I was screaming into my Goodreads updates, but seriously Tessa!! <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_m9wknfOYhJ1rzhv5ho1_500_zpshg7l7biu.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420347635ra/13207664.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m9wknfOYhJ1rzhv5ho1_500_zpshg7l7biu.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is the point when things start getting really screwy and my heart was racing out of my chest, I mean we have seen betrayal before and I really didn’t think I would see anything that would have me totally flabbergasted again…! I was crying angry tears for Tessa, I had to put the book down and walk away from it for a bit… I was in total and absolute disbelief…<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_m6sszfxspw1ql141xo1_500_zpsd08vyh3u.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420348031ra/13207704.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6sszfxspw1ql141xo1_500_zpsd08vyh3u.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_m2rxgjTkEv1r5ruse_zpsofdjaolr.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420348031ra/13207705.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m2rxgjTkEv1r5ruse_zpsofdjaolr.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/1giphy_zpse0a5thvm.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420348427ra/13207759.gif" alt=" photo 1giphy_zpse0a5thvm.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t want to give you tooo many details but just know that there is drama, frat house drama, Tessa’s dad drama, Tessa’s mother drama oh! and if you didn’t guess it? Yeah, there is plenty of Zed drama! <br>I mean I get it Zed is hot, he is nice, he shows up at the right time and at the right place but come on Tessa!!!! How much more are you going to push Hardin? Again I found myself wanting to slap some sense into this girl.<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/ec3f84ebe7_1398687338_Doe-je-dit-niet-Dan-verdien-je-een-klap-in-je-gezicht_zpsoqvlk9zf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420348908ra/13207813.gif" alt=" photo ec3f84ebe7_1398687338_Doe-je-dit-niet-Dan-verdien-je-een-klap-in-je-gezicht_zpsoqvlk9zf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In After We Fell, like After We Collided, we have Hardin’s POV which again is crucial to the story because while he still makes you mad you can understand why he is the way he is. I cant deny the growth in him, trying to control his temper, trying not to be impulsive and especially being much more considerate with Tessa, even his relationship with Landon makes you smile in this book. Again you see the wonderful guy he can be if he can learn to love himself. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/1Hanna-Caleb-hanna-and-caleb-20138201-500-270_zpsjqm5gjsm.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420352931ra/13208491.gif" alt=" photo 1Hanna-Caleb-hanna-and-caleb-20138201-500-270_zpsjqm5gjsm.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But, it’s Hessa we are talking about here so drama doesn’t stay at bay for too long and the last part of the book will prove to be jaw dropping totally unexpected drama, and for this I won’t drop even a hint because you really need to experience this for yourself. All I can say is that it was unexpected and devastating, I’m scared for Hardin and his state of mind and him falling into that downward spiral he seems to often flirt with. What he will face will definitely be a very tough pill to swallow. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/wtf-caleb_zpsovhy03jz.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420349901ra/13207936.gif" alt=" photo wtf-caleb_zpsovhy03jz.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The last line in this book left me hyperventilating and in disbelief… <br><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/51584-sheldon-breathing-in-a-paper-b-tq3z_zpswyc9l7x6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350335ra/13208015.gif" alt=" photo 51584-sheldon-breathing-in-a-paper-b-tq3z_zpswyc9l7x6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/6627176_zpsqy8xbmlv.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350421ra/13208064.gif" alt=" photo 6627176_zpsqy8xbmlv.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and in need of wine.. lots and lots of wine... <br><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_lsv95jzb2y1qgpz6j_zpsa9bri8yt.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350335ra/13208016.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lsv95jzb2y1qgpz6j_zpsa9bri8yt.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/elaine-chugging_zpsidimlmgj.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350335ra/13208017.gif" alt=" photo elaine-chugging_zpsidimlmgj.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/2under2wine_zpsyiioiinw.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350335ra/13208018.gif" alt=" photo 2under2wine_zpsyiioiinw.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It has been a very long time since I've had a book hangover, years even. I finished After We Fell and couldn't stop thinking about it, let alone start another book right away. <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/anigif_enhanced-buzz-22695-1377312605-4_zpsfaewddwl.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350907ra/13208125.gif" alt=" photo anigif_enhanced-buzz-22695-1377312605-4_zpsfaewddwl.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_n2wrzq3TJA1sgca9wo1_500_zpse8gy8vb3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350907ra/13208126.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n2wrzq3TJA1sgca9wo1_500_zpse8gy8vb3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The fourth and final installment will be hitting shelves on February 24, yup that's 50 days from today (but who's counting), I can totally wait, because I'm so not dying to know what happens next.... <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_inline_nd2s0snfRV1seifo9_zpsblykolyh.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350907ra/13208127.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_nd2s0snfRV1seifo9_zpsblykolyh.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>AAAAHHHHH! Who am I kidding!!? <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/I%20want%20it%20now_zps0pzggvzd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420350907ra/13208128.gif" alt=" photo I want it now_zps0pzggvzd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Thanks again to Gallery Books and Simon and Schuster for providing me with review copies, you guys are the best! <br><br>Here is something fun I'd like to share, I have been reading these books at the same time as some of my friends (we are all just as addicted to it), so when we all started of course updates were expected often<br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/tumblr_mtzujrDTW71rkiuhro1_500_zpsqftiq1l1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br>here is a small sample of our convos as we were reading After We Fell LOL <br><a href="http://s30.photobucket.com/user/Ursula_Uriarte/media/Untitled-1_zps81a8a7fe.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/918018101?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara" href="/user/show/14563697-sara">Sara</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer918018101" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13456578692320339705">WATTPAD VERSION! <br/><br/>I gave it two stars.<br/>I have nothing against the author. She's a respectful, kind hearted person. But I wasn't a huge fan of the writing and plot. The whole book is sex that in my opinion wasn't great. The book's plot was eh... But I don't want to hate. It's getting turned into a movie so congrats for the author, but I was just thinking that there are better books on wattpad that aren't fan fic that deserve to get promoted as much as After. I mean it's a fan fic, we should think a</span>
  <span id="freeText13456578692320339705" style="display:none">WATTPAD VERSION! <br /><br />I gave it two stars.<br />I have nothing against the author. She's a respectful, kind hearted person. But I wasn't a huge fan of the writing and plot. The whole book is sex that in my opinion wasn't great. The book's plot was eh... But I don't want to hate. It's getting turned into a movie so congrats for the author, but I was just thinking that there are better books on wattpad that aren't fan fic that deserve to get promoted as much as After. I mean it's a fan fic, we should think about that, wattpad shouldn't promote a fan fic so much, cause now wattpad is known for mostly fan fics. It's likes a fan fic website now. But anyway, the book has a lot of success, so congrats again to the author. I mean, even though it's not so greatly written and it's a fan fic, the author still got all the success!!! Which is great for her &lt;3<br />Bottom line, the book isn't so great, I couldn't make myself continue to read it cause it was not nicely written (I'm like a grammar nazi when it comes to books haha) I also got bored, and there was a lot of drama that didn't make sense and not a strong consistent plot. But I'm not hating, it's my honest opinion and I'm trying to be respectful about it. No disrespect to the author, but this is goodreads and your suppose to put a honest (respectful) review of books and that's exactly what I'm suppose to do. Whoever wants to read After obviously can but my review shows what it's about. A one direction fan fic, and its cliche, and has a lot of sexual scenes in it, and the plot and writing isn't strong. Anyway whoever decides to read this, well I hope you enjoy it cause hey, people have different tastes and I personally was not a fan of After. But all the best to Anna Todd, she really is a great person :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="13456578692320339705" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4748038-jaye-berry?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4748038-jaye-berry?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4748038-jaye-berry?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4748038-jaye-berry?shelf=2019">2019</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2777369481" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11311129565875265733">No series will ever come close to this one. The levels of problematic content and just being all around shitty in general? Go home everyone, this is it. One Direction did not deserve this.<br/><br/>I'll try to keep this brief because I've already murdered brain cells and wasted time on this god-awful series. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2774807903' rel='nofollow noopener'>My review for the last book pretty much sums up everything, even this book.</a> Hilariously this book really does just keep repeating itself and repeating itself but this time the page count is 848 pages!</span>
  <span id="freeText11311129565875265733" style="display:none">No series will ever come close to this one. The levels of problematic content and just being all around shitty in general? Go home everyone, this is it. One Direction did not deserve this.<br /><br />I'll try to keep this brief because I've already murdered brain cells and wasted time on this god-awful series. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2774807903" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for the last book pretty much sums up everything, even this book.</a> Hilariously this book really does just keep repeating itself and repeating itself but this time the page count is 848 pages! Are you serious? NOTHING happens in this book. The plot moves ahead maybe 15 pages and that count is just me being nice. You'd think in any of those useless filler pages she could write something at least semi-decent but no. Not a single moment is good but of course still as toxic and gross as ever. Quick shout-out to the attempted rape scene in the middle of the book that is still all about Hardin.<br /><br />This book is: Tessa and Hardin fight over something stupid (aka most of the time just his jealously and how much of an insecure baby he is), he screams and this time she tells him she needs a break. Yeah you can bet how well that works out. Hint, not very well. None of this drama is even a little interesting and it's just so exhausting to read their constant fights, and Hardin still being a super violent, controlling, and all around a piece of shit. I honestly can't believe this is book 3 out of over two thousand pages and we are STILL DOING THE SAME GODDAMN THING??<br /><br />This entire relationship is still the perfect example of abuse. It's amazing how well Anna Todd was able to show such a toxic and abusive relationship with all the signs you need to stay away from. I can't believe this series ever got published. It honestly makes me sick that this book is marketed as a "romance" and they think it would be good for anyone to read, let alone teenagers. This is not romantic, this is not goals. If you are in a relationship like this, please get help.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.rainn.org/" rel="nofollow noopener">RAINN</a><br /><a href="https://www.thehotline.org/" rel="nofollow noopener">National Domestic Violence Hotline</a></span>

I still loved the ending and i just keep reading so in a way i still lik</span>

But this is going on for like sooo long now. Even when you are in love, you know the right choice is to stop seeing eachother. But yeah, even though i'm annoyed. I still loved the ending and i just keep reading so in a way i still like it and give it 3 stars. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Z4d496KBXNofFxvc3mKUBfIY6L2hsriv85cqw+n6dMEqWCkuoATxGdB540R8kZDc6AaSO5COoa3NgQpxYZu0Ow==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TSrnAglMEHC5xBYNv6JP0kXlr5AW88E1cZGyToRo9C8A9bbbC8m9s3aq7pUdUUsLX/vVFifP2DdPh5L8DAk01Q==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer677134803650533254">ANNA TODD (Author/Writer/Producer) is the New York Times bestselling author of the After series of books, The Spring Girls, and the recent The Brightest Stars.<br/> <br/>Always an avid reader, Todd began writing stories on her phone on Wattpad, the reading and writing multiplatform for original stories, with After becoming its most-read series with over 1.5 billion reads. <br/> <br/>The print edition of After was pub</span>
  <span id="freeText677134803650533254" style="display:none">ANNA TODD (Author/Writer/Producer) is the New York Times bestselling author of the After series of books, The Spring Girls, and the recent The Brightest Stars.<br /> <br />Always an avid reader, Todd began writing stories on her phone on Wattpad, the reading and writing multiplatform for original stories, with After becoming its most-read series with over 1.5 billion reads. <br /> <br />The print edition of After was published in 2014 by Simon &amp; Schuster and has since been released in over 30 languages with more than 11 million copies sold worldwide. After has been a #1 bestseller across the globe including Italy, Germany, France and Spain. She has since written eight additional novels and serves as a producer and screenwriter on the upcoming film adaptation of After We Collided, the sequel to After. <br /> <br />Todd has been hailed by Cosmopolitan as “the biggest literary phenomenon of her generation.” A native of Ohio Anna, her husband and son currently live in Los Angeles.<br /> <br />Find her at AnnaTodd.com, on Twitter at @annatodd, on Instagram at @annatodd, and on Wattpad as Imaginator1D.<br /><br />Sign up for her mailing list for all the latest news: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://eepurl.com/cEm5e9">http://eepurl.com/cEm5e9</a><br />For more information on Anna Todd visit her website: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.annatodd.com/">http://www.annatodd.com/</a></span>
